12591460af max.yang 2020-09-02

AOS-304: Support to show red warning screen for secure build

  For secure build behavior:
    1. When device unlock, show red warning instead
    2. When uboot fail to valid AB slot, show red warning
    3. After 30s of red warning, device should shutdown
    4. red warning array is generate by command and modify array name:
        bmp_logo --gen-bmp lib/verifiedstate_idt/red_warning.bmp > red_warning_data.c
    5. red_warning.bmp put into codebase for anyone who need to adjust.

Change-Id: I6216ea744ad21e934766f04978ffa6dd505125a4

diff --git a/lib/verifiedstate_idt/idt_red_warning.c b/lib/verifiedstate_idt/idt_red_warning.c
new file mode 100644
index 0000000000..e810ffaeda
--- /dev/null
+++ b/lib/verifiedstate_idt/idt_red_warning.c
@@ -0,0 +1,80 @@
+/*
+ * Copyright (C) 2019 ID Tech
+ */
+
+#include <linux/types.h>
+#include <linux/delay.h>
+#include <command.h>
+#include <idt_red_warning.h>
+
+#ifdef CONFIG_AVB_WARNING_LOGO
+#include "lcd.h"
+#include "video.h"
+#include "dm/uclass.h"
+#include "fsl_avb_logo.h"
+#include "video_link.h"
+#include "video_console.h"
+#include "video_font_data.h"
+#endif
+
+void idt_show_red_warning_and_shutdown(void)
+{
+#ifdef CONFIG_AVB_WARNING_LOGO
+	int ret = 0, count = 0;
+	struct udevice *dev;
+
+	ret = uclass_first_device_err(UCLASS_VIDEO, &dev);
+	if (!ret) {
+		/* clear screen first */
+		video_clear(dev);
+#ifdef CONFIG_IDT_ROTATION
+		/* Draw the red warning bmp logo */
+		ret = bmp_display((ulong)red_warning_logo_bitmap,
+					CONFIG_AVB_WARNING_LOGO_COLS, CONFIG_AVB_WARNING_LOGO_ROWS,
+					false);
+#else
+		ret = bmp_display((ulong)red_warning_logo_bitmap,
+					CONFIG_AVB_WARNING_LOGO_COLS, CONFIG_AVB_WARNING_LOGO_ROWS);
+#endif
+		/* Show warning text. */
+		if (uclass_first_device_err(UCLASS_VIDEO_CONSOLE, &dev)) {
+			printf("no text console device found!
");
+			return;
+		}
+		/* Adjust the cursor postion, the (x, y) are hard-coded here. */
+		vidconsole_position_cursor(dev, CONFIG_AVB_WARNING_LOGO_COLS/VIDEO_FONT_WIDTH,
+						CONFIG_AVB_WARNING_LOGO_ROWS/VIDEO_FONT_HEIGHT + 6);
+		vidconsole_put_string(dev, "No valid operating system could be found");
+		vidconsole_position_cursor(dev, CONFIG_AVB_WARNING_LOGO_COLS/VIDEO_FONT_WIDTH,
+						CONFIG_AVB_WARNING_LOGO_ROWS/VIDEO_FONT_HEIGHT + 7);
+		vidconsole_put_string(dev, "The device will not boot");
+		/* Jump one line to show the link */
+		vidconsole_position_cursor(dev, CONFIG_AVB_WARNING_LOGO_COLS/VIDEO_FONT_WIDTH,
+						CONFIG_AVB_WARNING_LOGO_ROWS/VIDEO_FONT_HEIGHT + 13);
+		vidconsole_put_string(dev, "Visit this link on another device:");
+		vidconsole_position_cursor(dev, CONFIG_AVB_WARNING_LOGO_COLS/VIDEO_FONT_WIDTH,
+						CONFIG_AVB_WARNING_LOGO_ROWS/VIDEO_FONT_HEIGHT + 14);
+		vidconsole_put_string(dev, "g.co/ABH");
+
+		vidconsole_position_cursor(dev, CONFIG_AVB_WARNING_LOGO_COLS/VIDEO_FONT_WIDTH,
+						CONFIG_AVB_WARNING_LOGO_ROWS/VIDEO_FONT_HEIGHT + 20);
+		vidconsole_put_string(dev, "PRESS POWER BUTTON TO SHUTDOWN...");
+		/* sync frame buffer */
+		video_sync_all();
+
+	} else {
+		printf("no video device found!
");
+	}
+
+	/* Block at this screen for 30s and shutdown */
+	while ((count < 10 * CONFIG_AVB_WARNING_TIME_LAST) && !is_power_key_pressed()) {
+		mdelay(1000);
+		count++;
+	}
+	do_poweroff(NULL, 0, 0, NULL);
+
+#else   /* CONFIG_AVB_WARNING_LOGO */
+	/* UUU no need, just return */
+	return;
+#endif
+}
